# NHNProject
nhn 사전 과제

# Install
- [Python 3.10.6](https://www.python.org/downloads/release/python-3106/)
- [SQLite3](https://sqlitebrowser.org/dl/)

# Requirements
```bash
$ pip list
Package              Version
-------------------- -----------
beautifulsoup4       4.11.1
Django               4.1.5
djangorestframework  3.14.0
lxml                 4.9.2
mysqlclient          2.1.1
pip                  22.3.1
pytz                 2022.7.1
requests             2.28.2
selenium             4.7.2
webdriver-manager    3.8.5
```

# Project Setup
```bash
# 파이썬 설치 필수

# git clone
$ git clone https://github.com/jihye0420/NHNProject.git <프로젝트 이름>

# 가상환경 생성
$ cd NHNProject
$ python venv .venv

# 가상환경 활성화
$ source .venv/bin/activate  # 맥
$ source .venv/Scripts/activate  # 윈도우

# Then install the dependencies
$ (.venv)$ pip install -r requirements.txt

# Django settings
(.venv)$ python manage.py makemigrations
(.venv)$ python manage.py migrate

# 크롤링 시작
(.venv)$ python crawling.py

# API 호출
(.venv)$ python manage.py runserver
```

### 입력 : [http://127.0.0.1:8000/group/10](http://127.0.0.1:8000/group/10)

조건<br/></p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(1) 해당 분야에 전문적인 능력을 가진 자 또는 자격증 소지자</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(2) 직무 수행의 결격사유나 학생 지도 시 건강에 이상이 없는 자</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(3) 방과후학교 개인위탁 외부강사 활동에 제한이 없는 자</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">1. 제출 서류<br/></p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(1) 방과후학교 프로그램 운영 제안서 1부[서식1]</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(2) 자기소개서[붙임1]</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(3) 프로그램 운영 제안서[붙임2]</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(4) 경력증명서</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">1. 기타사항<br/></p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(1) 제출된 서류 및 평가내용은 반환하거나 공개하지 아니함</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(2) 제출된 서류 및 기재사항이 허위로 드러날 경우 선정 및 계약을 무효로 함</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(3) 1차 서류전형 실시 후 적격자가 없을 경우 재공고 할 수 있음</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">(4) 문의 전화 : 031-8020-1304 (교무실)</p><p style=\"text-align: left;\">1. 11. 16.<br/></p><p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>용 인 초 등 학 교 장</strong></p>",

</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi\" id=\"SE-70415205-6e9e-4d19-b494-8ceb41bd7a31\" style=\"color:#000000;\"><b>모든 미취업 청년을 대상으로 하며, 1회 100만 원 이내 실비를 지원합니다.</b></span><span 교통카드'(G-PASS 카드)를 발급받아 충전해야 합니다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi\" id=\"SE-c5833150-5bc9-4364-872a-97954439cf47\" style=\"color:#000000;\"><b>시는 이 카드로 결제된 버스 이용요금을 3개월 단위로 정산해         "title": "노후 소각시설 민간투자 대체 건립 2026 준공 등",

이슈 ◎</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs24 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-ba3ccc64-4c84-4fa9-bd49-809b6252ade1\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>성남시, '지역 멘토가 알려줌' 참여 희망 취준생 80명 모집</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-ed673d66-c14c-401c-9a3d-19cfe6ae99eb\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>경기 성남시는 오는 21일까지 '지역 멘토가 알려줌(ZOOM)' 행사 참여를 희망하는 취업 준비생 80명을 모집한다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-913596b3-ded2-4cc2-b3d5-07d36ab41e8a\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>이 행사는 매칭된 SK C&amp;C 기업인(16명)을 온라인 화면으로 만나 관심 직무 분야에 관해 물어보고, 궁금증을 푸는 멘토링 방식으로 진행된다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-c70bdff6-4662-464a-bc3e-d57fc8f0b221\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>직무 멘토링은 오는 27일 시스템 개발, 웹·앱 개발, 총무, 재무 등 16개 분야에서 이뤄진다. 각 분야 멘토(기업인) 1명에 멘티(취준생) 5명이 매칭된다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-b8428890-8c10-4b0d-8b68-7d04f171e94e\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>취업 준비 과정과 성공전략, 실무 현장에서 하는 일, 직무 정보와 비결 등 다양한 소재로 소통할 수 있다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-93bd28ad-daf9-4faa-b91f-3dd7563c9290\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>대학생, 취업 준비생 등 만 19~39세 청년은 기한 내 성남시 평생학습 포털 배움숲을 통해 선착순으로 신청하면 된다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-69c65ab8-ba3b-4662-9551-21e65d1e6174\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b>멘티로 선정되면 성남시가 행사 당일 온라인 화상 플랫폼(Zoom) 주소를 보내준다.</b></span><span se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-8a71097b-ccd9-478c-a4ea-4c65eab4c153\" style=\"color:#000000;background-color:#ffffff;\"><b> </b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" ‘생활폐기물처리시설 민간투자사업 시행자 지정 및 실시협약’을 체결했다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-9a706b39-534d-4cfb-9e37-c1a7107c4915\" 부담금 350억원 등 총 1585억원이다.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs-fs19 se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset\" id=\"SE-f5328f78-b28a-4829-a094-6f1bef295d79\" class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-d9baf0f9-e8e0-4047-9098-10358ccdc60a\" style=\"color:#0044ff;\"><b>요양, 돌봄 등 고령자 맞춤형 주거복지 서비스를</b></span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-ce7c3070-4d52-4424-b180-834dc545f7fd\" style=\"color:#0044ff;\"><b>종합적으로 지원 중이야.</b></span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-b7849e91-f105-4653-ba3f-82f0b9d1d0a0\" style=\"\">오늘의 딱풀이, </span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-60bb53d5-ddd3-4c19-90bd-964af5f48922\" style=\"\">자세하고 알기 쉽게 설명해 줄게!</span><span class=\"se-fs-fs28 se-ff-\" id=\"SE-692ee403-8879-424d-a539-4c0497738521\" id=\"SE-3b4b07eb-6b76-4298-924e-d151486c3580\" style=\"\">거주하는 주택에서 멀지 않은 곳에</span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-1438924c-eb82-4245-b9b9-c251949583e3\" style=\"\">복지관이 있기 때문에, </span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-dba8f01f-80eb-4309-862a-aedc4a0ab78e\" style=\"\">어르신들의 건강, 식사 등을 </span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-e2690a91-a765-488c-8821-e79131555ae5\" style=\"\">수시로 확인할 수 있는 장점이 있어.</span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-3087916f-16f8-483a-8d67-a2abc1e1e33f\" style=\"\">또한, 경로당·경로식당·다목적실 등 </span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-60cd47a5-9cc2-4a9e-9534-f74f0905f30e\" style=\"\">다양한 시설과 더불어 </span><span class=\"se-fs- se-ff-\" id=\"SE-cccfcd7d-1eaa-4eee-ba24-ba731f269c5b\" style=\"\">건강교육, 우울증 및 치매 예방 프로그램을         "url": "https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-64364143?at_medium=RSS&at_campaign=KARANGA",
        "title": "First woman pastor in Holy Land ordained",
        "published_datetime": "2023-01-22T14:44:52Z",
        "body": "<p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\"><b class=\"ssrcss-hmf8ql-BoldText e5tfeyi3\">In many parts of the Christian world, female church leaders are no longer unusual. But until now, the Holy Land - where events in the Bible are set - had not seen a local woman ordained.</b></p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">On Sunday, a Palestinian from Jerusalem, Sally Azar, became its first woman pastor at an event at the Lutheran church in the heart of the Old City, attended by hundreds of international well-wishers.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"I got more excited seeing the excitement of other people,\" Reverend Azar told me. \"It's an indescribable feeling to take this step with the support of the church.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"I hope that many girls and women will know this is possible and that other women in other churches will join us. I know it will take a long time, but I think it could be exciting if this changes in Palestine.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Christians make up a minority in the Palestinian Territories, Israel and Jordan. Most Christians here belong to the Greek Orthodox and Latin Catholic Churches, which do not allow women priests.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">However, the ordination of women has been taking place in a growing number of Protestant Churches in the past few decades. These have small local congregations and run schools and hospitals in the Holy Land.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"Everywhere where you have a patriarchal society and culture this is a major step,\" says the recently retired Archbishop of the Church of Sweden, Antje Jackelen.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"Since I've been ordained for over 40 years, I've met many people who didn't think it was possible. But now they've seen women actually serving as pastors, as bishops, as archbishops, we know it works and we know that it's actually in accord with the Bible.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">In the Middle East, churches in Lebanon and Syria have already conferred holy orders on women, while at least one Palestinian woman is known to serve in the US.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Ms Azar was ordained by her father Bishop Sani Azar. She insists that while his example inspired her, she never felt pressured into studying theology.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"It's what I wanted, what I was called to do,\" she says.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">As a pastor she will take on different duties including leading services and bible studies in Jerusalem and in Beit Sahour, in the occupied West Bank, for English speaking congregations.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"It's a big, big day for the life of our Church, it's an important step forward and it's overdue,\" comments Reverend Dr Munther Isaac, Lutheran Pastor of Bethlehem and Beit Sahour. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He says he looks forward to introducing Reverend Azar as a role model at local Lutheran schools - which teach children who are Christians of all traditions and Muslims.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Rev Dr Isaac has written a book in Arabic about women's leadership in the Bible and in support of women's ordination.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"We accept women ministers, we accept women professors, we accept to go in surgery performed by women and it's strange that we still have to argue that women can teach the Bible or perform the sacraments,\" he says.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"This tells me that despite the progress we've made as Palestinians, when it comes to empowering women and women rights, that there is still work to be done.\" </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Supporters of Rev Azar believe she is the right person to challenge stereotypes and break the mould.</p>",
        "attachment_list": []

        "url": "https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-64362640?at_medium=RSS&at_campaign=KARANGA",
        "title": "Call for probe into claim BBC chair helped ex-PM secure loan",
        "published_datetime": "2023-01-22T14:44:25Z",
        "body": "<p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\"><b class=\"ssrcss-hmf8ql-BoldText e5tfeyi3\">Labour is calling for a parliamentary investigation into claims the chairman of the BBC helped Boris Johnson secure a loan guarantee, weeks before the then-PM recommended him for the role.</b></p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\"><a class=\"ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0\" href=\"https://www.thetimes.co.uk/article/the-bbc-chairman-the-prime-minister-and-the-800-000-loan-guarantee-f7nt5kfml\">The Sunday Times says</a> Richard Sharp was involved in arranging a guarantor on a loan of up to Â£800,000 for Mr Johnson.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Mr Sharp said he had \"simply connected\" people and there was no conflict of interest.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Mr Johnson's spokesman said he did not receive financial advice from Mr Sharp.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He also dismissed Labour's suggestion Mr Johnson could haveÂ breached the code of conduct for MPs \"through failing to appropriately declare the arrangement\" on his Parliamentary register of interests.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Labour's chairwoman Anneliese Dodds has written to the Parliamentary Commissioner for Standards, Daniel Greenberg, asking for \"an urgent investigation into the facts of this case\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Foreign Secretary James Cleverly told the BBC's Laura Kuenssberg that \"of course perception matters\". But he added Mr Sharp was an \"incredibly accomplished, incredibly successful individual\", and there was \"no doubt he was appointed on merit\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He also said it was not \"unusual for someone to be politically active prior to their appointment to senior BBC positions\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Mr Sharp declined to appear on Laura Kuenssberg on Sunday but told the show \"the claim that there was anything financial involved is not true\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Meanwhile, Mr Johnson travelled to Ukraine on Sunday to visit parts of Kyiv and meet with President Zelensky.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Mr Johnson was reported to be in financial difficulty in late 2020.  </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The Sunday Times says multimillionaire Canadian businessman Sam Blyth - a distant cousin of Mr Johnson - raised with Mr Sharp the idea of acting as Mr Johnson's guarantor for a loan. It is not clear where the loan agreement itself came from.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Mr Sharp - a Conservative Party donor who at the time was applying to be the chairman of the BBC - contacted Simon Case, the then-cabinet secretary and head of the civil service. The paper says a due diligence process was then instigated. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The Cabinet Office later wrote a letter telling Mr Johnson to stop seeking Mr Sharp's advice about his personal finances, given the forthcoming BBC appointment, the Times says.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">BBC News has not seen the letter and the Cabinet Office said it would \"not comment on private discussions between any prime minister and officials\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">According to the paper, Mr Sharp, Mr Blyth and Mr Johnson had dinner together at Chequers before the loan guarantee was finalised, although they deny the PM's finances were discussed then.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Former Goldman Sachs banker Mr Sharp was announced as the government's choice for the new BBC chairman in January 2021. The role is recommended by the culture secretary and the prime minister.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The BBC chairman heads the board that sets the corporation's strategic direction and upholds its independence. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The Sunday Times says candidates for such publicly-appointed roles are required to declare any conflicts of interest. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">In a statement, Mr Sharp said: \"There is not a conflict when I simply connected, at his request, Mr Blyth with the cabinet secretary and had no further involvement whatsoever.\" </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Labour had already written to the Parliamentary Commissioner for Standards calling for an investigation into the reports Mr Blyth had set up the loan guarantee.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The guarantee is a promise by one party - known as a guarantor - to assume the debt obligation of a borrower if that borrower defaults.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">In her letter to the commissioner, Ms Dodds cites the Sunday Times story, saying she was concerned that Mr Johnson may have breached rules \"by asking for an individual to facilitate a guarantee on a loan whom he would later appoint to a senior public role\". </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">She said that a \"lack of transparency\"  may \"give the impression that this was a quid pro quo arrangement, something which would undermine the integrity of the democratic process, and calls into question the process by which the chairman of the BBC was appointed\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Shadow culture minister Lucy Powell has also sent a letter to the Commissioner for Public Appointments to look into the selection process for the chair of the BBC. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">She wrote: \"It is vital that the public and Parliament can have trust in this process and it is free from any real or perceived conflict of interest.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">A spokesman for Mr Johnson said: \"Richard Sharp has never given any financial advice to Boris Johnson, nor has Mr Johnson sought any financial advice from him. There has never been any remuneration or compensation to Mr Sharp from Boris Johnson for this or any other service. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"Mr Johnson did indeed have dinner with Mr Sharp, whom he has known for almost 20 years, and with his cousin. So what? Big deal. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"All Mr Johnson's financial arrangements have been properly declared and registered on the advice of officials.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">A BBC spokesman said: \"The BBC plays no role in the recruitment of the chair and any questions are a matter for the government.\"</p>",

        "title": "'Get it all out now' over tax affairs, Zahawi urged",
        "published_datetime": "2023-01-22T14:26:59Z",
        "body": "<p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\"><b class=\"ssrcss-hmf8ql-BoldText e5tfeyi3\">Nadhim Zahawi should release \"the absolute facts\" on his tax affairs after paying a settlement with HMRC, former Conservative Party leader Sir Iain Duncan Smith has said.</b></p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Tory party chairman Mr Zahawi has faced mounting pressure over claims he tried to avoid tax and had to pay it back.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">On Saturday the ex-chancellor said he had paid a settlement and HMRC had accepted it was a \"careless\" error.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Labour said the matter had been \"corrosive to public trust\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Asked on <a class=\"ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0\" href=\"https://www.bbc.co.uk/iplayer/episode/m001hhxb/sunday-with-laura-kuenssberg-22012023\">Sunday with Laura Kuenssberg</a> if it would be better for Mr Zahawi to publish everything that had happened relating to his tax affairs, Sir Iain said \"the sooner you can get the absolute facts out the better\", rather than it \"coming out in phases.\"</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He said he would say to Mr Zahawi to \"get it all out now whatever you have to do and clear it up\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">But he defended Mr Zahawi, saying he \"genuinely\" did not believe he was \"deceitful\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Foreign Secretary James Cleverly said it was for Mr Zahawi to decide \"how much detail to put in the public domain\". </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">According <a class=\"ssrcss-k17ofw-InlineLink e1no5rhv0\" href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/uk-news/2023/jan/20/nadhim-zahawi-agreed-on-penalty-to-settle-tax-bill-worth-millions\">to the Guardian,</a> Mr Zahawi had to pay back tax he owed with a 30% penalty, the total amounting to Â£4.8m.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The BBC has been unable to verify that figure, but when the paper asked about the penalty, Mr Zahawi's spokesperson did not deny one had been paid. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">This weekend Mr Zahawi issued a statement saying he wanted to address \"confusion about my finances\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He did not make clear whether or not he had paid a penalty as part of his settlement, nor did he say how much he had paid to HMRC. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\"> Mr Zahawi said when he was being appointed chancellor, questions were being raised about his tax affairs and he had discussed it with the Cabinet Office at the time.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">An aide to Mr Zahawi confirmed to the BBC that the tax matter was resolved while he was serving as chancellor.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">On Sunday, the foreign secretary was asked about what he knew about the circumstances surrounding Mr Zahawi's tax affairs.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">He said he did not know if Mr Zahawi had sorted out his settlement with HMRC while he was chancellor, nor if he had paid a penalty as part of a settlement, nor if this was all discussed with the prime minister.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Labour's deputy leader Angela Rayner called on Rishi Sunak to \"come clean on what he knew and when\" about Mr Zahawi's tax affairs.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">The case \"is corrosive to public trust, with a chancellor in charge of the nation's finances asking the public to pay their taxes while apparently having failed to do so himself,\" Ms Rayner said.</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">She added it was the prime minister's responsibility to \"decontaminate his scandal-ridden cabinet by setting out clearly what steps he has taken to ensure that all ministers' tax affairs are in order\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">Speaking to the BBC, Labour's shadow chancellor Rachel Reeves said she \"would be happy\" to publish her own tax returns \"if that was the thing that was necessary\".</p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">In the statement issued on Saturday afternoon, Mr Zahawi said: \"As a senior politician I know that scrutiny and propriety are important parts of public life. </p><p class=\"ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph eq5iqo00\">\"Twenty-two years ago I co-founded a company called YouGov. I'm incredibly proud of what we achieved. # 설명

1. 크롬 드라이버 설정 ⇒ 설치하지 않아도 되는 코드를 작성했다.
    
    ```python
    def get_driver():
        # 구글은 분당 4회이상 접근 허용하지 않기 때문에 sleep을 길게 준다.
        # time.sleep(2)
    
        chrome_options = Options()
        # chrome_options.add_argument("headless")
        driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=Service(ChromeDriverManager().install()), options=chrome_options)
        return driver
    ```
    
2. 중복 데이터를 확인하는 로직 설정
    
    ```python
    def insert_data_db(category, crawled_data_list):
        # item = crawled_data_list[0]
        for item in crawled_data_list:
            print("item", item)
            if Post.objects.filter(category=category, url=item['url'], title=item['title']).exists():
                print('중복')
                print(Post.objects.filter(category=category, url=item['url'], title=item['title']).first())
                continue
            else:
                print('insert')
                Post(url=item['url'],
                     title=item['title'],
                     published_datetime=item['published_datetime'],
                     body=str(item['body']),
                     attachment_list=",".join(item['attachment_list']),
                     category=category).save()
        return
    ```
    
3. 크롤링 timezone 설정 로직 추가 ⇒ UTC 기준으로 insert되도록 설정했다.
    
    ```python
    def convert_to_date_utc(category, pub_date):
        if type(pub_date) == str:
            if category == 'iam_school':
                pub_date = datetime.strptime(pub_date, '%Y.%m.%d')  # 문자열을 출력
                kst = pytz.timezone('Asia/Seoul')
                kst_time = kst.localize(pub_date)
                pub_date = kst_time.astimezone(pytz.utc)
            elif category == 'naver_blog':
                pub_date = datetime.strptime(pub_date, '%Y. %m. %d. %H:%M')  # 문자열을 출력
                kst = pytz.timezone('Asia/Seoul')
                kst_time = kst.localize(pub_date)
                pub_date = kst_time.astimezone(pytz.utc)
            elif category == 'bbc_news':
                pub_date = datetime.strptime(pub_date, '%a, %d %b %Y %H:%M:%S %Z')
                utc = pytz.timezone('UTC')
                pub_date = utc.localize(pub_date)
        return pub_date
    ```
